SAMPLE     The diameter of the sample was usually about 0.5 in.   11626  1   13 
           With this size of sample, the resolution figures       11626  1   14 
           ranged downward from about 8 nsec/m for a mean energy  11626  1   15 
           of 5 keV to about 2 nsec/m, for a mean energy of 45    11626  1   16 
           keV. All samples were in the form of pressed metal or  11626  1   17
